***screech.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a> (41579)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>1602; altered with expressive vowel lengthening from earlier <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">skrech</i> (1577), variant of obsolete <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scritch</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">skriken</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">shrichen</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">schrichen</i> (1250), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_English" class="extiw" title="w:Old English">Old English</a></span> (attested as <i class="Latinx mention" lang="ang">scriccettan</i>) and <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skríkja</i>, both from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skrīkijaną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Icelandic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Icelandic language">Icelandic</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="is">skríkja</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Saxon" class="extiw" title="w:Old Saxon">Old Saxon</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="osx">scricōn</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="da">skrige</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skrika</i>), derivative of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*skrīhaną</i> (compare <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">schriën</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/German_language" class="extiw" title="w:German language">German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="de"><a href = vnd.unilang:schreien.html>schreien</a></i>, Low German dial. <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">schrien</i>, <i class="Latn mention" lang="nds-de">schriegen</i>), ultimately of imitative origin.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a></strong> (<i>countable and uncountable</i>, <i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">screeches</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A high-pitched strident or piercing sound, such as that between a moving object and any surface.</li>
<li>A harsh, shrill cry, as of one in acute pain or in fright; a shriek; a scream.
<ul><li><b>1826</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Mary_Shelley" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:Mary Shelley"><a href = vnd.unilang:mary.html>Mary</a> Shelley</a>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Last_Man" class="extiw" title="wikipedia:The Last Man">The Last <a href = vnd.unilang:man.html>Man</a></a>, volume 3, chapter 6
<dl><dd>That the night owl should <b>sreech</b> before the noonday sun, that the bat should wheel around the bad of beauty [...]</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">Newfoundlander<span class="ib-comma">,</span> uncountable</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> Newfoundland <a href = vnd.unilang:rum.html>rum</a>.</li>
<li>A form of home-made rye <a href = vnd.unilang:whiskey.html>whiskey</a> made from used oak rye <a href = vnd.unilang:barrels.html>barrels</a> from a distillery.</li></ol>
<h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<div class="NavFrame">
<div class="NavHead" style="text-align: left;">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></div>
<div class="NavContent derivedterms" style="text-align: left; column-count: 2; -moz-column-count: 2; -ms-column-count: 2; -o-column-count: 2; -webkit-column-count: 2;">
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a> bird</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">screecher</span></li></ul>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a> hawk</span></li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a> owl</span></li></ul>
</div></div>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screech.html>screech</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en">screeches</b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">screeching</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">screeched</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To make such a sound.
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2004</b> April 15,  “Morning swoop in hunt for <a href = vnd.unilang:jodi.html>Jodi</a>'s killer”, in  <cite>The Scotsman</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.scotsman.com/news/morning_swoop_in_hunt_for_jodi_s_killer_1_521912">[1]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">AS THE residents of the quiet Midlothian housing estate prepared for the day ahead, the early-morning stillness <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> disturbed by the sound of <b>screeching</b> brakes and slamming <a href = vnd.unilang:doors.html>doors</a>.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">intransitive<span class="ib-comma">,</span> figuratively</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> to travel very fast, as if making the <a href = vnd.unilang:sounds.html>sounds</a> of brakes being released
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>2011</b> December 12,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sid.html>Sid</a> Lowe,  “Víctor Valdés epitomises Barcelona's bravery as Real Madrid falter”, in  <cite>the Guardian</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://www.guardian.co.uk/football/blog/2011/dec/12/victor-valdes-barcelona-real-madrid?INTCMP=SRCH">[2]</a></sup>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">You've got to admire their <a href = vnd.unilang:balls.html>balls</a>. Real Madrid <b>screeched</b> after them: an entire herd, powerful and co-ordinated, salivating and breathing hard, murder in their <a href = vnd.unilang:eyes.html>eyes</a>. So Barcelona moved the ball on, away from them. Forced back, it <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> played into Víctor Valdés, the goalkeeper, who slotted it to Carles Puyol, who <a href = vnd.unilang:gave.html>gave</a> it back again.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li></ol>

<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">screen</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">saver</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:screensaver.html>screensaver</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">screensavers</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">software</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A computer program that <a href = vnd.unilang:displays.html>displays</a> aesthetic patterns or images when the computer <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> not being used, originally intended to prevent screenburn.
<dl><dd><i>I configured my <b><a href = vnd.unilang:screensaver.html>screensaver</a></b> to appear after only two minutes, because I enjoyed watching it so much.</i></dd></dl></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">proscribed</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> The background picture of a computer, smartphone, or similar mobile device.

***scull.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a> (21798)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_English" class="extiw" title="w:Middle English">Middle English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="enm">sculle</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">a type of oar</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, of uncertain origin, possibly from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/North_Germanic_languages" class="extiw" title="w:North Germanic languages">North Germanic</a></span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Norse" class="extiw" title="w:Old Norse">Old <a href = vnd.unilang:norse.html>Norse</a></a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="non">skola</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">to rinse, wash</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup>
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sculls.html>sculls</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li>A single oar mounted at the stern of a boat and moved from side to side to propel the boat forward.</li>
<li>One of a pair of oars handled by a single rower.</li>
<li>A small rowing boat, for one person.</li>
<li>A light rowing boat used for racing by one, two, or four rowers, each operating two oars (<a href = vnd.unilang:sculls.html>sculls</a>), one in each hand.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">racing boat</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span><span class="ib-colon sense-qualifier-colon">:</span> <span class="Latn" lang="en">double <a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">quad <a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></span>, <span class="Latn" lang="en">single <a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></span></li></ul>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sculls.html>sculls</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sculling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sculled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li>To row a boat using a <a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a> or <a href = vnd.unilang:sculls.html>sculls</a>.
<ul><li><b>1908</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Kenneth_Grahame" class="extiw" title="w:Kenneth Grahame">Kenneth Grahame</a>, <i><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/The_Wind_in_the_Willows" class="extiw" title="w:The Wind in the Willows">The Wind in the Willows</a></i>
<dl><dd>The afternoon sun <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> getting low as the <a href = vnd.unilang:rat.html>Rat</a> <b>sculled</b> gently homewards in a dreamy mood, murmuring poetry-things <a href = vnd.unilang:over.html>over</a> to himself, and not paying much attention to Mole.</dd></dl></li></ul></li>
<li>To skate while <a href = vnd.unilang:keeping.html>keeping</a> both <a href = vnd.unilang:feet.html>feet</a> in contact with the ground or ice.</li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Derived_terms_2">Derived <a href = vnd.unilang:terms.html>terms</a></span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>
<ul><li><span class="Latn" lang="en">sculler</span></li></ul>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_2">Etymology 2</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>See <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">skull</i>. The verb sense may derive from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Danish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Danish language">Danish</a></span>/<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Norwegian_language" class="extiw" title="w:Norwegian language">Norwegian</a></span>/<span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Swedish_language" class="extiw" title="w:Swedish language">Swedish</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="sv">skål</i>.
</p>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun_2">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sculls.html>sculls</a></b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="form-of-definition use-with-mention">Obsolete form of <span class="form-of-definition-link"><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">skull</i></span></span>.</li>
<li>A skull cap. A small bowl-shaped helmet, without visor or <a href = vnd.unilang:bever.html>bever</a>.
<ul><li><b>1786</b>, <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Francis_Grose" class="extiw" title="w:Francis Grose">Francis Grose</a>, <i>A Treatise on Ancient Armour and <a href = vnd.unilang:weapons.html>Weapons</a></i>, page 11.
<dl><dd>The <b><a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> a head piece, without visor or <a href = vnd.unilang:bever.html>bever</a>, resembling a bowl or bason, such as <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> worn by our cavalry, within twenty or thirty years.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Verb_2">Verb</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:scull.html>scull</a></strong> (<i>third-person singular simple present</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en 3 | s | pres-form-of" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:sculls.html>sculls</a></b>, <i>present participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en pres | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sculling</b>, <i>simple past and past participle</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en past | and | past | ptcp-form-of" lang="en">sculled</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Australia" class="extiw" title="w:Australia">Australia</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/New_Zealand" class="extiw" title="w:New Zealand">New Zealand</a><span class="ib-comma">,</span> <a href = vnd.unilang:slang.html>slang</a></span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> To <a href = vnd.unilang:drink.html>drink</a> the entire contents of (a drinking vessel) without pausing.
<ul><li><b>2005</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:jane.html>Jane</a> Egginton, <i>Working and Living Australia</i>, The Sunday Times, Cadogan Guides, UK, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=wcCrVckSnN4Camp;pg=PA1998amp;lpg=PA1998amp;dq=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22+australia+OR+beer+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=u3SLqyF4JNamp;sig=T2bPfc3zOp4ukBjJlJuE_aGwo-8amp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=5zw6UL-1B46XiAfXkYCgDQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22%20australia%20OR%20beer%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 59</a>,
<dl><dd>In 1954, <a href = vnd.unilang:bob.html>Bob</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:hawke.html>Hawke</a> made the <i>Guinness Book of Records</i> for <b>sculling</b> 2.5 pints of <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> in 11 <a href = vnd.unilang:seconds.html>seconds</a>.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2005</b>, Stefan Laszczuk, <i>The Goddamn <a href = vnd.unilang:bus.html>Bus</a> of Happiness</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=EM_ThcG_XJECamp;pg=PA75amp;lpg=PA75amp;dq=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22+australia+OR+beer+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=bboiT53rrNamp;sig=SYXDcK8kpSi-HPHYFl_WNrv0Oagamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=5zw6UL-1B46XiAfXkYCgDQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22%20australia%20OR%20beer%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 75</a>,
<dl><dd>That way you get your opponent so gassed up from <b>sculling</b> <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> that all he can think about <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> trying to burp without spewing.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2006</b>, Marc Llewellyn, Lee Mylne, <i>Frommer′s Australia from $60 a Day</i>, 14th Edition, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=1fJoPZ4d3m4Camp;pg=PA133amp;lpg=PA133amp;dq=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22+australia+OR+beer+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=P64za2qJhCamp;sig=JY4OiWtrUaHteMYvJhgAenVxvaAamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=5zw6UL-1B46XiAfXkYCgDQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22%20australia%20OR%20beer%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 133</a>,
<dl><dd>For a livelier scene, head here on Friday or Saturday night, when mass <i>beer-<b>sculling</b></i> (chugging) and yodeling are accompanied by a brass <a href = vnd.unilang:band.html>band</a> and costumed waitresses ferrying foaming <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a> steins about the atmospheric, cellarlike space.</dd></dl></li>
<li><b>2010</b>, <a href = vnd.unilang:matt.html>Matt</a> Warshaw, <i>The History of Surfing</i>, <a rel="nofollow" class="external text" href="http://books.google.com.au/books?id=HTL8tumsVB0Camp;pg=PA136amp;lpg=PA136amp;dq=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22+australia+OR+beer+-intitle:%22%22+-inauthor:%22%22amp;source=blamp;ots=5-yQcvRBrnamp;sig=F7xT26hd9Du3nGNSi0T7grXK3rcamp;hl=enamp;sa=Xamp;ei=5zw6UL-1B46XiAfXkYCgDQamp;redir_esc=yv=onepageamp;q=%22sculled%22%7C%22sculling%22%20australia%20OR%20beer%20-intitle%3A%22%22%20-inauthor%3A%22%22amp;f=false">page 136</a>,
<dl><dd>After a three-day Torquay-to-Sydney road trip with his hosts, Noll rejoined his American temmates, unshaven and stinking of alcohol, the Team USA badge ripped from his warm-up jacket and replaced by an Aussie-made patch of Disney character Gladstone <a href = vnd.unilang:gander.html>Gander</a> <b>sculling</b> a frothy mug of <a href = vnd.unilang:beer.html>beer</a>.</dd></dl></li></ul></li></ol>
<h5><span class="mw-headline" id="Synonyms">Synonyms</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h5>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:scumbag.html>scumbag</a> (67543)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><i class="Latn mention" lang="en">scum</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">bag</i>
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="en"><a href = vnd.unilang:scumbag.html>scumbag</a></strong> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-en p-form-of" lang="en">scumbags</b>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">vulgar<span class="ib-comma">,</span> dated</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> condom
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1978</b>,  <a href = vnd.unilang:sonia.html>Sonia</a> Pilcer,  <cite>Teen Angel</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="http://books.google.com/books?ei=ATkZTpfwEImssAOfj4nnDQamp;id=a1uxAAAAIAAJ">[1]</a></sup>, <small>→ISBN</small>:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">“A <b><a href = vnd.unilang:scumbag.html>scumbag</a></b>,” <a href = vnd.unilang:sonny.html>Sonny</a> repeated. “Rubber. A <i>pro-phy-natic</i>. You know what I mean, don'<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a> you?”</span></div></dd></dl></div></li></ul></li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">mildly vulgar</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> sleazy, disreputable or despicable person; lowlife
<ul><li><div class="citation-whole"><span class="cited-source"><b>1953</b> July 19,  <a href = vnd.unilang:allen.html>Allen</a> Cromley,  “Report from Washington”, in  <cite>The Daily Oklahoman</cite> | <sup><a rel="nofollow" class="external autonumber" href="https://www.newspapers.com/clip/22746515/scumbag_from_1953/">[2]</a></sup>, Oklahoma City, <a href = vnd.unilang:ok.html>Ok</a>, page 1:</span><dl><dd><div class="h-quotation"><span class="Latn e-quotation" lang="en">Monroney <a href = vnd.unilang:was.html>was</a> variously described as a "<a href = vnd.unilang:scumbag.html>scumbag</a>," "SOB," "Snake," "dead sheep," ... and assorted unprintable adjectives.</span></div></dd></dl></div></li>
<li><div class="h-usage-example"><i class="Latn mention e-example" lang="en">Can you believe that <b><a href = vnd.unilang:scumbag.html>scumbag</a></b> <a href = vnd.unilang:steve.html>Steve</a> asked to sleep with her before <a href = vnd.unilang:even.html>even</a> asking her name?</i></div></li></ul></li></ol>

***secondant.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:secondant.html>secondant</a> (38939)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/French_language" class="extiw" title="w:French language">French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fr"><a href = vnd.unilang:secondant.html>secondant</a></i>. Equivalent to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">seconderen</i> + |  <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">-ant</i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secondant.html>secondant</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="masculine gender">m</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secondanten.html>secondanten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secondant.html>secondantje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A <span class="Latn" lang="en">second</span>, a prominent aide or assistant, chiefly one who <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> left in charge when a superior <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> absent.</li>
<li>A <span class="Latn" lang="en">second</span> <span class="gloss-brac">(</span><span class="gloss-content">attendant of a <a href = vnd.unilang:duel.html>duel</a> or boxing match standing in for a contestant</span><span class="gloss-brac">)</span>.</li>
<li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">historical</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> A second teacher, one substituting a headteacher when necessary <span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content qualifier-content">chiefly used for former times when schools frequently <a href = vnd.unilang:had.html>had</a> only one or a few teachers</span><span class="ib-brac qualifier-brac">)</span>.</li></ol>
<hr />
<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Zelfstandig_naamwoord"><i><a href = vnd.unilang:zelfstandig.html>Zelfstandig</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:naamwoord.html>naamwoord</a></i></span></h4>
<p><b><a href = vnd.unilang:secondant.html>secondant</a></b> <span style="background-color: f8f9fa;border-radius: 2px;border: 1px solid c8ccd1;padding: 0 0.2em 0 0.1em;font-style: italic">m</span> <sup id="cite_ref-3" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-3"> | 3 | </a></sup>
</p>
<ol><li><a href = vnd.unilang:iemand.html>iemand</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:die.html>die</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:een.html>een</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:ander.html>ander</a> <a href = vnd.unilang:steunt.html>steunt</a> of <a href = vnd.unilang:bijstaat.html>bijstaat</a></li></ol>
</body>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:secreet.html>secreet</a> (34698)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum"><a href = vnd.unilang:secreet.html>secreet</a></i>. <span class="maintenance-line"><i>This etymology <a href = vnd.unilang:is.html>is</a> incomplete. You can help Wiktionary by elaborating on the origins of this term.</i></span>

<hr><h4><span class="mw-headline" id="Noun">Noun</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h4>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secreet.html>secreet</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secreten.html>secreten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secreet.html>secreetje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>outhouse</li>

<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secretariaat.html>secretariaat</a></strong> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span> (<i>plural</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl p-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secretariaat.html>secretariaten</a></b>, <i>diminutive</i> <b class="Latn form-of lang-nl diminutive-form-of" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:secretariaat.html>secretariaatje</a></b> <span class="gender"><abbr title="neuter gender">n</abbr></span>)
</p>
<ol><li>a central office in any business or institution (or a department thereof), responsible for correspondence, making appointments, and general administrative support</li>
<li><span class="Latn" lang="en">secretariat</span></li></ol>

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Medieval_Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Medieval Latin">Medieval Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēcrētārius</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">one entrusted with <a href = vnd.unilang:secrets.html>secrets</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēcrētus</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">private, secret</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, <a href = vnd.unilang:perfect.html>perfect</a> passive participle of <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēcernō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I separate; I part; I reject</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sē-</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">apart</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> + <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">cernō</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">I separate, sift</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>.

***sedert.html
<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sedert.html>sedert</a> (22424)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">tsedert</i>, a variant form of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sedert.html>sedert</a></i> (pronounced with initial <i>z-</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Middle Dutch">Middle Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">seder</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">thenceforth, since then</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>. Originally a Hollandic dialectal form, the other dialects used <i class="Latn mention" lang="dum">sider</i> (which would have become modern <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl">*sijder(<a href = vnd.unilang:t.html>t</a>)</i>), from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_Dutch" class="extiw" title="w:Old Dutch">Old Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="odt">sīther</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīþiz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss"><a href = vnd.unilang:later.html>later</a></span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, a comparative form of <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sīþuz</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">late</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span> (from which the <a href = vnd.unilang:rare.html>rare</a> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zijd.html>zijd</a></i>). Ultimately related to <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sinds.html>sinds</a></i>.
</p>
<hr><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Preposition">Preposition</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p><strong class="Latn headword" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:sedert.html>sedert</a></strong>
</p>
<ol><li><span class="ib-brac">(</span><span class="ib-content">dated or formal</span><span class="ib-brac">)</span> since

<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Middle_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Middle High German">Middle High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="gmh">sēr</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_High_German" class="extiw" title="w:Old High German">Old High German</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="goh">sēr</i> <span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">(</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">“</span><span class="mention-gloss">sored, injured</span><span class="mention-gloss-double-quote">”</span><span class="mention-gloss-paren annotation-paren">)</span>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Proto-Germanic_language" class="extiw" title="w:Proto-Germanic language">Proto-Germanic</a></span> <i class="Latinx mention" lang="gem-pro">*sairaz</i>. Cognate with <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/English_language" class="extiw" title="w:English language">English</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="en">sore</i>, <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Dutch_language" class="extiw" title="w:Dutch language">Dutch</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zeer.html>zeer</a></i>.

</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:sein.html>sein</a> (11009)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology_1">Etymology 1</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>From <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Old_French" class="extiw" title="w:Old French">Old French</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">seigne</i>, a northern variant of <i class="Latn mention" lang="fro">signe</i>, from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">signum</i>.<sup id="cite_ref-1" class="reference"><a href="cite_note-1"> | 1 | </a></sup> Doublet of <i class="Latn mention" lang="nl"><a href = vnd.unilang:zegen.html>zegen</a></i>.
</p>

<head> <meta charset='utf-8'> </head> <body><h1> <a href = vnd.unilang:seminarie.html>seminarie</a> (18720)</h1><br><h3><span class="mw-headline" id="Etymology">Etymology</span><span class="mw-editsection"></span></h3>
<p>Borrowed from <span class="etyl"><a href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Latin" class="extiw" title="w:Latin">Latin</a></span> <i class="Latn mention" lang="la">sēminārium</i>.
